msg:The environment of the hotel is really very good. The lobby has a very nice fragrance and a landscape terrace. The room is also quite large, and the bed is also relatively large among the hotels I have stayed in. The room facilities are very new. The design of the induction light in the cloakroom is very anti-human, because the cloakroom does not have an open door, but its induction light design is not limited to the occasion. As long as there is a movement of passing by, it will light up. So, when other people in the room rest at night, someone gets up to go to the toilet in the middle of the night and passes by the cloakroom, it will light up. This light is not like a night light mode, but a normal full-on light. Can you bear it?
Service: Because it was during the May Day holiday, the front desk said when checking in that it was full, so no extra bed or bedding could be added. This is understandable, but it has been clearly stated that there are two adults and two children, and no toiletries for the children, no bathrobes and slippers, etc. I called on the first day and sent a children's bathrobe. Starting at 8 pm on the second day, I called for a children's bathrobe. During the period, I urged three or four times, and they said they were sending it, but as of the third day of check-out, I did not receive the bathrobe that was being sent. In addition, the next day after the first night, we went out to play after breakfast. When we came back, we found that the crabs that the children caught the day before (in a milk tea cup) were gone! The small bottle of facial cleanser on the washstand was gone! I have stayed in other hotels before. Even if I left a worn-out shoe on the floor of the room, I would be called to ask if it was a missing item and whether it needed to be sent back.
The swimming pool is quite large and everyone cleans it, but the security guard played with his mobile phone the whole time.
When checking in, a guest at another counter said that he called at 9 o'clock in the morning and asked for an extra bed. At that time, he promised that it was possible. As a result, he was told that it could not be added in the afternoon because it was out of use. I don't know if the coordination was completed in the end.
In summary, the hotel's hardware is very good, and there is still a lot of room for improvement in service.

msg:The hotel is very new. I checked in during the Spring Festival. I had to wait a little while to check in. It is understandable. Because I was on a different floor from the elderly, the hotel is more private. When I swipe the room card, the elevator will automatically press the floor, so I made another door card in the end to facilitate the companionship.
The hardware is very good, smart toilet, cloakroom, everything you need, but the makeup mirror will automatically go down, and the person who puts on makeup has to hold it with his hand, which may be the case in my room.
There is a park near the hotel, which is more like a large green space.
The service of the housekeeping depar**ent is good, and the things you need can be delivered immediately. The boss will take the initiative to greet you when you go out.
The breakfast is not bad, but this hall is actually not big. You may have to queue up for a seat when you encounter a peak meal. There are not many varieties of food, that is, there are both Chinese and Western food, but not many varieties.
The shortcoming is that the air conditioning is not very powerful. Because it was suddenly hot during the Spring Festival, the air conditioning has not been able to cool down after it was turned on.
When I arrived by car, I had a lot of luggage, but the hotel staff at the door were completely indifferent. Yes, they just watched you pull the luggage down from the car with difficulty, just watching. You can't make yourself unhappy during the Spring Festival, so you move it yourself.
The parent-child afternoon tea is provided with the room reservation. Both rooms are parent-child rooms, so there are two servings. When we arrived at the lobby, the staff was very busy. After confirming the order, we sat down and packed it for us. We wanted to finish eating in the lobby and go back to the room, but there were two take-away bags. Forget it, we had to go back to the room.
For takeout, we ordered three times in total, milk tea and sushi, and finally picked them up by ourselves. We saw the robot, but it never delivered it. Because it was too hot, the takeaway guy didn't deliver the sushi for half an hour, so we had to pick it up again. The previous milk tea was almost the same. We saw that the two robots were completely non-operating. The takeaway was delivered to the counter at the front desk. There was no service staff at the counter. There were actually 4-5 other takeaways on the counter. 7:30 to 8 pm. There was a shortage of staff during the Chinese New Year. I hope it will be improved later.
